NID 6 is 'AnonymousPro-Bold', Everything looks good.

Anonymous Pro Bold Italic (AnonymousPro-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'AnonymousPro-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Anonymous Pro Bold Italic (AnonymousPro-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'AnonymousPro-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Do gray = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

Info

subtable

head

(head table lowestRecPPEM is '9')
